The Wanbaoshan Case in a Standoff

▲ Zhong Yu Returns to Harbin and Speaks to Reporters

▲ Withdrawal of Police is Only One of the Preliminary Issues

▲ No Negotiations on Any Other Issues Have Been Held Yet

Harbin Correspondence: Zhong Yu, under orders from the central government, has been negotiating the Wanbaoshan case in Jilin for almost a month. On the morning of the 14th, he returned to Harbin for business and will return to Jilin in a week to continue negotiations with Japanese Consul Ishii. In the past few days, Wang Jiazhen has been in Harbin, and he has been busy with social engagements. Reporters have visited him several times without success. It was not until 11:00 AM on the 16th that he was finally received. When asked about the progress of the Wanbaoshan case negotiations, he spoke as follows:

I have been away from Harbin for almost a month, traveling back and forth between Jilin and Liaoning to seek instructions and to meet with Japanese Consul Ishii. The negotiations are currently in a standoff, with no hope of progress in the near future. I am returning to Harbin for a few days to deal with urgent official matters, as I have been away for some time. I will have to return to Jilin in a week to continue negotiations. When I left Jilin, I instructed Director Shi (Luban) of the Jilin office to immediately telegraph me if he received any notification from the Japanese Consul, so that I could go there. These negotiations are more difficult because the Japanese side insists that local negotiations should be casual, and each meeting does not adhere to diplomatic norms. Regardless of whether it is related to the case or not, they simply engage in idle talk. I have met with them more than ten times, without adhering to diplomatic customs. Several times we sat and talked for eight or nine hours, from morning to evening, without even stopping to eat. Our side has consistently maintained that (1) the withdrawal of Japanese police from Majiashao and (2) the departure of Koreans from the Wanbaoshan area are preliminary matters for this negotiation. If these two matters cannot be resolved, then there is no need to discuss the issues of the case itself. The Japanese side insists that the Japanese police cannot withdraw until the case has

Page 11

Summary of Important News

been resolved. If they withdraw, they must (1) still allow Koreans to reside in the Wanbaoshan area and must make every effort to protect them, (2) ensure that the ditches and dams at Majiashao are not damaged, so that rice can be planted and water can be drawn next year. There are many other conditions, but in short, they insist on not withdrawing immediately. On one occasion, they even demanded the leveling of the ditches and the installation of water pipes, claiming that this would be to avoid damaging farmland. I refused all of these requests. Ishii had no choice but to consult his Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which replied that our Ministry of Foreign Affairs' first note contained the words "withdrawal of Japanese police, departure of Koreans, pending resolution," which was almost a command. If they were to comply, it would inevitably appear that they knew they were wrong and were showing submission. The Ministry instructed Ishii not to comply. After several more discussions, the Japanese Consul finally obtained instructions from his Ministry of Foreign Affairs, allowing the withdrawal of police, but there was no need to publish any documents, and the Japanese police would withdraw automatically and unconditionally. At the same time, Koreans would be free to move as they please, and the ditches and dams would not be leveled for the time being. Our side would unconditionally advise farmers not to riot during this period, pending negotiations. However, Changchun Japanese Consul Tashiro at this time was still unwilling to withdraw police. After Ishii negotiated with him several times, he finally agreed, and the 26 Japanese police withdrew on August 8. Before leaving, they demolished a section of the dam to release the upstream water. As for the Koreans, they will also be leaving the country in the next few days. Such is the current situation of the case negotiations. The conversations between me and Ishii reported in various newspapers are purely fabricated, because I have never made any statements to the outside world, and Ishii also agreed not to publish anything in the newspapers until a result is reached. The reports in the outside world are clearly fabrications. I have already sent letters to the newspapers to correct them. Regarding the previous negotiations, both sides have kept records as a basis for future discussions. In short, although the Japanese police have withdrawn, negotiations are just beginning. There will be many difficulties in future negotiations, because Japan considers the Wanbaoshan case to be related to its entire New Continent colonization policy, and therefore will not relax in the slightest on negotiations. (16th)

Rumors arose for a time, and people were panicked, foreshadowing a major crisis in the future. The generals all understand the great righteousness, love the country, and love their hometowns, and have always been enthusiastic. Deleted and printed by the Shanxi Provincial Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party." Beiping Correspondence: There has been a lot of talk about Yan and Feng going abroad, but in fact, it is still far from reality. Overview of the Dangerous Situation of the Yellow River in Shandong Province

▲ Important Dangerous Works Are Everywhere

▲ The Downstream Water Level Has Risen Another Foot

Jinan Correspondence: The water level of the Yellow River this year is high, and in the 22 counties along the river, in the upper, middle, and lower reaches, extending no less than seven or eight hundred li, important dangerous works are everywhere, almost impossible to prevent and impossible to rescue. The source of the water is still strong. Yesterday, the 19th, the River Affairs Bureau specially reported all the dangerous works on the entire river to the Provincial Government. The original text is as follows: "To Shandong Provincial Government Chairman Han Jun: According to urgent telegrams from the second, third, fifth, sixth sections in the north and the second, third, and fourth sections in the south, the sudden change in the flow of the Wulongtan People's Embankment in the second section in the north, the collapse of the top of the second dam embankment, over ten zhang long; the seventh and eighth stone dykes in Qiaozhuang in the third section in the north collapsed by one or two zhang; the third stone dam in Wangzhuang, the second and twenty-sixth stone dams in Xijia Daokou, successively collapsed by one or two zhang; the lower corners of the fourth and fifth gray stone dikes in Tangjia and Changjia in the fifth section in the north collapsed; the eighth dam in Wangjiaji was submerged; the front of the fourth dam, the lower corner of the fifth dam, and the middle of the twelfth dam in Liujiakou all collapsed by more than one zhang; the entire dam of the third dam in Dacui collapsed; three dykes of the tenth dam in Mazhangjia were eroded by over six zhang; the dikes and dams in Gongjia, Sunjia, Damajia, Qijiazui, Wangzhuang, etc., in the sixth section in the north all rose in the water by one or two chi, and the erosion is constantly occurring; the lower corner of the twentieth stone retaining wall in Huojia Liu in the second section in the south collapsed; the upper and lower corners of the twenty-first dyke in Chenjiaquan were submerged; the seventh, ninth, and fourteenth stone dams in Luokou were all flooded; the upper corner of the fifth dam collapsed by two zhang; the base of the Da Daowang dyke dam collapsed by over one zhang; six sections of the Majia Ping Dyke Dyke, eight sections of Daoxu, thirteen sections of Fengjia, nineteen sections of Wang Wangzhuang, ten sections of Zhoujia Overwater Dyke Dyke, five sections of Xiaowangzhuang, and four sections of Fotousi have all been submerged. The situation of the work is dangerous and precarious. In addition to telegraphed orders to the section chiefs of the respective areas to lead their troops and civilians, regardless of wind, rain, day, or night, to spare no effort to rescue and protect them to ensure safety, I respectfully report. Director of the River Affairs Bureau Zhang Lianjia respectfully kowtows."

According to veterans of river affairs, the Yellow River in the upper reaches of this province is as wide as thirty li, while the lower reaches are as narrow as one li. The water that rose three chi and four cun in Shaanxi on the 17th had already been seen in the upper reaches on the morning of the 19th, so the water level rose again by one chi and two cun. When the water reaches the lower reaches, where the river is narrower, the water level will definitely increase. A telegram has already been received from the upper reaches, reporting an emergency, "To Jinan River Affairs Bureau and directors of all bureaus in the middle and lower reaches, Chief of Qing River Section Liang Junjian, from yesterday (18th) evening to this (19th) morning, the river water has risen by over one chi, totaling over eight chi with the previous rise. The dangerous works in Sunjia and Damajia are critical, and the flow is fierce. All the dykes and dams are completely submerged, with depths of two, three, or four chi. The flow on the dykes is eroding the base of the dams and splitting the top of the embankments, making them extremely dangerous. It is necessary to mobilize more civilians to strengthen the rescue efforts to ensure safety. A letter has been sent to the magistrate of Lijin County, ordering him to immediately dispatch 500 police and civilians to the embankment to assist, but fearing that the process will be slow and not timely, troops have been ordered to the embankment to urgently mobilize 200 civilians with gongs. The seat is requested to come to the works to instruct on the situation. Kowtows waiting for orders. Also, the works at Gongjiaba, Qijiazui, Wangzhuang, etc., are also critical at the same time. The county magistrate of Lijin has been instructed to dispatch civilians separately to assist in the rescue. Respectfully reported, Zheng Rong, Di Jibaoren kowtow." (20th)

Jiangbei Flood Investigation Notes (Too Late)

Between late summer and autumn, continuous rain for weeks has caused flooding in more than ten provinces of our country, with the Jiangbei region of Jiangsu Province suffering the most severe disaster. The unique reasons include its low-lying terrain, adjacent to Gaoyou, Shaobo, and Hongze Lakes, which have long been known as a land of marshes. In addition, the former course of the Yellow River upstream and the waters of the Huai and Yi Rivers overflow downwards, causing the Grand Canal to overflow. The vastness of Taihu Lake in Jiangnan and the increasing water level of the Yangtze River, block both upstream and downstream areas. The Gaobao area resembles a water tank, with its water level higher than the rivers and lakes. Only a long dike that has been neglected for many years is holding it back. Consequently, the earthen levees have been breached, and the land has been turned into a vast ocean, with the people scattered and displaced, and agricultural activities completely submerged. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented in decades. The Jiangsu Flood Relief Association entrusted me to inspect the area for a week. I took a steamer and sailed against the waves, directly reaching Qingjiangpu.

Qinghuai is a place I have visited before, and I have many old friends there. This time, I came to survey the disaster, so I did not visit them. The Xiaoshui Gate and the North Gate were both blocked with earthen embankments. Suddenly, news came that the two sluice gates had collapsed, causing widespread panic. In reality, both gates had double-hole breaches (a culvert was in danger of collapsing). The Gaosheng Bridge was submerged, with a breach measuring twelve feet wide and ten feet deep, flooding into the Chaimihe River. Local people held emergency meetings one after another, requesting the Huaipi Engineering Office to open the Shuangjin gate panels. The Liang General Headquarters also sent a special task force to deal with the emergency. The water reached Xiaojie Street in the South Gate (according to reports, the water in the South Gate was partly caused by the pressure of Gaoyou and Hongze Lakes, and not entirely from the breach). I saw countless disaster victims repairing the old camps and levees as a temporary measure to escape the water. Outside the city, a vast expanse of water submerged crops, carried away livestock, and destroyed houses and graves. The exact number of deaths could not be determined. It is estimated that more than 20,000 to 30,000 households are currently homeless and awaiting death. At Hejiaxiang, south of the Grand Canal and outside the Dongwei Gate, the dike collapsed the day before yesterday. For a time, people supporting the old and carrying the young created a clamorous noise. Li Junwan, the head of Sanjiang Township, gathered the people by sounding a gong, and about 500 people joined the emergency repair effort. Fortunately, a major disaster was averted.

The next day, I rode a donkey to Huaicheng, about thirty li away. Along the riverbank, there were some newly repaired sections. West of Huai, from Gaoliangjian to the west dike of the Grand Canal, and from Yangjiamiao to the Taiping South Dike, there were dozens of li in each direction. The polder fields only yielded one autumn harvest. Due to the rising water of Hong Lake, it moved eastward with force, and the waters of Baima Lake and the Grand Canal were full and unable to discharge. The poor people had no seeds or seedlings, and most of them lived in nests in trees. The bodies of people and animals floated on the surface of the water in the newly constructed riverheads of Bafang. The heartbreaking scene is beyond description.

From Huaicheng to Baoying, passing through Erpu Pingqiao, about eighty li, I took a boat downstream. The water was high, and the boat sailed like an arrow. Looking west to the Great Lake, it was a boundless expanse of white. The earthen dike was almost level with the water, and the lake fields had become a marshland. Countless elderly and weak people drowned. Those who had not drowned but escaped were all living on the west bank of the river, dwelling in mat sheds, winding for dozens of li, serving as the only place of refuge for the disaster victims. Wives held their husbands, and children carried their mothers, appearing emaciated and eager for food. Looking east, the isolated city of Baoying was like sitting at the bottom of a pot, in imminent danger of falling. The Grand Canal dike was intermittent, with newly added earthen berms that were no more than three feet wide. The water was only a little more than a foot below the berms, vast and extremely dangerous. Fortunately, the southeast wind had been blowing for days, allowing for the construction to continue with stone transport, additional materials, and soil pressing, with round-the-clock defense. If a northwest wind were to suddenly blow, the lake water would rise steeply by three to five zhang, creating a tidal wave, white waves reaching the sky, like mountains moving and seas overturning. The sand and stones would be swept away for more than a hundred li, and the counties of Yan, Fu, Tai, and Dongxing would all become marshlands connected to the sea. If there were an unforeseen event, the world would change again. The river disaster is actually more severe than the Yangtze River disaster. Preventing the disaster is most dangerous in Gaobao. If the river dike collapses, the damage could extend for thousands of li. Historical records in the Gaobao County Chronicle confirm this, and it is not an exaggeration.

From Baoying to Gaoyou, about one hundred and twenty li, the Grand Canal dike also has some newly repaired sections. The river water has already risen above the old dike, and the newly added loose soil and thin dike construction are also a cause for concern as they are eroded by the water.

That day, I stayed outside the county town at Yumatou. At midnight, the sound of gongs urging emergency repair and the wails of women and children were incessant. The farmers guarding the shore rose up to repair the breaches. Suddenly, the Wuliba was breached by the water. After the Sanba opened, the water level of the upper river was slightly lower than before, but the water level of the lower river suddenly rose by more than eight feet. The water broke through many embankments. The most tragic was Gaomiaowei, only a short distance from the dam, which bore the brunt of the disaster. The water reached the rooftops, drowning countless people and livestock. From the trees, one could still hear the cries of the living. The young and old, widows and orphans, either groaned by the roadside or wailed on both banks. The heartbreaking scene was unbearable to witness.

I took a mail boat south to Shaobo and disembarked. The dike had been newly repaired for about eight li. Because the water level had risen sharply before, a sub-dike had been added. Now that the water level continued to rise, the previous sub-dike had lost its ability to resist the water. As a result, three more feet were added to it in the following days (from the Nan Dawang Temple to the North Ban Factory). The water level at Sangu Shuizhi near Zhaoguan Dam rose to two zhang and two chi and five cun due to the increase in upstream flow. The water level was the highest on record. During this trip to various places, there was disaster victims everywhere, with tears in their eyes and choked voices.

Reaching Yangzhou, about forty li, the market near the customs house was flooded. The disaster was more severe in the Hongqiao area on the south side of the Yangtze River. San Gongwei, north of Guazhou Liuwei, collapsed the day before yesterday. The water was extremely strong, destroying more than 300 houses and submerging countless fields. The disaster victims scattered in all directions. The strong went to Jiangnan to find food, while the weak wandered in ditches and gullies. Their cries for help echoed back and forth in the waves and floods.

The disaster this year is widespread in size and scope. Even if the Sanba are opened together, it will not be easy to drain the water in a short time. If we consider the disaster situation in Jiangbei, Gaobao is the most severely affected. Because of its position on the shores of the lake, the fields and houses have been submerged, and people and animals have been displaced. If benevolent and kind people do not quickly rise up to rescue them, how will the tens of thousands of disaster-stricken people who have no clothes, no food, and no shelter survive?

Jiangsu Province Second Provincial Congress Elects Provincial Executive and Supervisory Committee Members

Zhenjiang correspondence: The Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress of Provincial Representatives held a general election of Provincial Executive Committee Members and Supervisory Committee Members at 2:00 PM on the 21st in the lecture hall of Baixian Park in Zhenjiang. 149 representatives were in attendance. The presidium publicly elected Huang Yuren as chairman. The Central Party Headquarters specially dispatched Wu Jiayou, the chief secretary of the Organization Department, as the election supervisor. After the chairman led the assembly in a ceremony and made a report, Wu Jiayou, the Central Election Supervisor, delivered a brief speech stating that the Jiangsu provincial party affairs in the past had a long and profound history, which was not only due to the efforts of all party members in the province, but also due to the effective guidance of the provincial party headquarters, which led to good results. The Congress has resolved many important cases, and the development of Jiangsu provincial party affairs in the future can be predicted. Today's election meeting hopes that all representative comrades will break through all emotional effects and elect comrades who have a historical, loyal, and responsible attitude in the party to take on the important task of provincial party affairs. This is not only the hope of the Central Government, but also the expectation of all comrades in the province. Following this, the chairman announced the election regulations and detailed election rules, which included the election of seven executive committee members, five alternate executive committee members, five supervisory committee members, and two alternate supervisory committee members. After the Central Election Supervisor verified the party certificates and credentials of each representative, the chairman appointed the staff of the meeting to distribute the ballots and begin the election. After the election, the ballot counters verified that the number of ballots matched the number of representatives present, and then opened the ballot box and announced the results. The number of executive and supervisory committee members elected was doubled and submitted to the Central Government for approval. The results are recorded below:

▲ Executive Committee Candidates (for Central Approval): Ma Yinbing 76 votes, Xie Chengyu 75 votes, Zhang Yuanyang 73 votes, Ye Xiufeng 69 votes, Yang Xingqin 65 votes, Qi Xiyong 64 votes, Huang Yuren 61 votes, Ni Bi 58 votes, Zhou Shaocheng 51 votes, Gu Ziyang 43 votes, Cao Minghuan 42 votes, Zhou Houjun 41 votes, Pan Guojun 33 votes, Zhang Renjie 33 votes, Chen Kanghe 29 votes, Cheng Ruyuan 25 votes, Zhu Yunji 20 votes, Lan Weibin 17 votes, Yu Huaizhong 15 votes, Ge Kexin 15 votes, Zuo Qipeng 14 votes, Xu Wenjun 12 votes, Zhao Yuzheng 12 votes, He Xuyou 12 votes.

▲ Supervisory Committee Candidates (for Central Approval): Ge Jianshi 106 votes, Duan Muzhen 71 votes, Zhou Yeren 53 votes, Qiu Youzhen 47 votes, Wang Gongyu 35 votes, Niu Changyao 33 votes, Zhang Minquan 33 votes, Zhou Butian 30 votes, Chen Sibai 29 votes, Wu Xiangshan 25 votes, Wang Zhenxian 24 votes, Zhou Fengjing 23 votes, Wu Baofeng 23 votes, Qi Shuzu 20 votes.

Jiangsu Province Second Provincial Congress Meeting Notes

▲ Numerous Important Cases Resolved on the 21st

▲ Requesting the Central Government to Punish Mu Bin, Sun Hongzhe, and Others

▲ Emergency Motion to Request the Central Government to Remove Lin Biao from Office

Yesterday (the 21st) was the seventh day of the Second Jiangsu Provincial Congress of Provincial Representatives. At 9:00 AM, the sixth general meeting was held. 78 representatives were in attendance. The presidium nominated Zhang Renjie as chairman. After leading the ceremony, Xu Wenjun, a member of the proposal review committee, reported. Following this, the proposals were discussed: (1) Proposal to promote party affairs work in this province (proposed by the Provincial Party Consolidation Committee), divided into: 1. Determining the central work of party affairs in this province within one year: (A) Guiding all district branches in the province to hold meetings on time and concentrating all party member activities in the district branches; (B) Formulating measures to improve the educational level of party members in this province; (C) Concentrating the work of district party headquarters and district branches to handle rural public education and propaganda of party doctrines; (D) Stipulating the work that party headquarters in each county in this province should carry out for local autonomy and the rights and responsibilities borne by party members; (E) Stipulating the strategies for party headquarters at all levels to guide the work of local people's organizations. 2. Determining the treatment standards and inspection methods for party affairs workers in this province. 3. Stipulating that party members should be coordinated and supervised by the senior party headquarters in their locality when serving the community. 4. Determining the period, methods, and standards for recruiting probationary party members in this province. Resolution: Passed in principle, and the review opinions were submitted to the Congress Secretariat to organize the text. (2) The former Jiangsu Provincial Director of Civil Affairs, Mu Bin, violated the law, betrayed the party, harmed the country and the people, and his evil deeds are well-known. The Congress should resolve to request the Central Government to expel him from the party, strictly arrest him according to the law, and purify party discipline (proposed by Suining representatives, co-signed by 50 representatives from various counties in Zhenjiang). The reasons are fourfold: employing the poor and corrupt, openly engaging in bribery, excluding dissidents and harming comrades, and plundering the people's wealth. Resolution: Passed. Measures: 1. Request the Central Government to expel Mu Bin from the party, order his arrest and bring him to justice, and confiscate all his stolen goods and turn them over to the public. 2. In addition to receiving party discipline, Mu Bin should also be handed over to the court to be tried for the crime of slander. 3. Request the Central Government to thoroughly investigate the unscrupulous party members who colluded with Mu Bin to harm comrades in our party. (3) Sun Hongzhe, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction, Mao Yisheng, Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, and Li Zhongqiang, Chief of the Gaobao Section, are ignorant of water conservancy and lack common sense of river engineering. They employed private individuals and neglected their duties, resulting in an unprecedented catastrophe, drowning countless people and animals, and turning houses into ruins, causing millions of people to starve to death. The severity of the disaster is unprecedented. We earnestly request the Congress to impeach them to show a warning and to appease public anger (proposed by representatives from Yancheng and other counties). Resolution: The Congress will request the Central Government to forward to the National Government a request to promptly dismiss Sun Hongzhe, Director of the Department of Construction, and punish him. The Provincial Government should also be consulted to promptly dismiss Mao Yisheng, Director of the Water Conservancy Bureau, and Li Zhongqiang, Chief of the Gaobao Section, and hand them over to the court for interrogation.

Emergency motion: Lin Biao, President of the High Court, should be given a serious warning for failing to attend the Congress to report on his work under the pretext of illness. Resolution: Submit to the Central Government a request to order the Ministry of Judicial Administration to remove Lin Biao from office.

Local Correspondence

Fengxian

The abduction and enticement of a maid, requesting a thorough investigation. Hu Musheng, a farmer from Xiahengjing, Songjiang, has a daughter named A Hui. Since childhood, she was betrothed to Zhang Atong of Tinglin as his wife. However, due to their poor family circumstances, at the age of twelve, she was pawned by Tang Heshang Niangniang of Zhuangxing for twenty yuan to Zhuang Zhihe of Nanqiao to work as a maid. It was agreed on three sides that the redemption date would be fifteen years. Unexpectedly, after the girl grew up, Zhuang saw her beauty and seduced her into an affair. Later, she was not tolerated by the first wife and was privately sold as a concubine to Dai Lanshi, who opened a lace company in Xiaoyouli, Xujiahui, Shanghai. After Dai died, she remarried Song Yinghe, a patrolman in Yangshupu, last year. Now, the girl's father, Hu Musheng, believes that the pawn period has expired, so he prepared the redemption price last month. When he arrived in Nanqiao, Zhuang had already moved to Shanghai. So he asked people everywhere to inquire about the news and finally learned the truth. The Zhuang family saw that Hu could be bullied and refused to admit it. Therefore, Hu had no choice but to hire a lawyer yesterday together with Zhang Atong, the girl's husband, to file a lawsuit to investigate.

Kunshan

The Provincial Order Prohibits Foreigners from Leasing Land. The Kunshan County Government previously received a letter from Pu Aide, the president of the Shanghai Yacht Club, requesting to permanently lease the riverside land along the Qingyang Port in this county to build a yachting venue for the club. Maps and previous contracts were attached. After receiving the letter, the county government believed that the matter was related to international territory and of great importance, so it reported the situation to the provincial government for instructions. Now, the provincial order states that Qingyang Port belongs to the interior and the request cannot be approved. After receiving the order, the county government has sent a reply to the club to inform them.

Songjiang

Inspector Yang cracks down on kidnappers. Kidnappings have occurred frequently in various townships of Fengjing. The Public Security Bureau strictly ordered Inspector Yang Shijie to arrest the perpetrators within a time limit. Today (the 21st), Inspector Yang cracked down on Zhang Yunting, the principal offender who kidnapped four members of Li Yuting's family in Fengjing for a ransom of 4,000 yuan, and two suspected accomplices, Xiang A'er, in a restaurant south of Changqiao in this city. They were sent to the Public Security Bureau for preliminary interrogation. According to Zhang Yunting, he had kidnapped two Tang family members in Qingpu territory in the 17th year [of the Republic], obtained funds for ransom, and so on. He was ordered to be detained pending verification.

County Magistrate Shen swears in. County Magistrate Shen Yong was transferred to Songjiang and has been here for a month. On the 21st, he held a supplementary swearing-in ceremony at the County Government's Haishitang. Yan Shenyu, the county magistrate of Shanghai, was appointed by the Provincial Office to supervise the oath.

Suzhou

Investigating the Situation of Grain Storage in Wuxian Charity Granaries. The Department of Civil Affairs sent Jiang Fuqin to Suzhou to investigate the Wuxian Charity Granaries and to investigate the flood situation at the same time. Regarding the flood problem, since the fields in the various townships are currently a vast ocean, there is no way to investigate. The investigation of the Charity Granaries has been completed. Yesterday (the 21st), it was reported to the Civil Affairs Office by the county government: (1) The current amount of securities and bills in the Charity Granaries is 20,742 yuan, 4 jiao, and 5 fen, with 500 yuan in interest, 8,970 yuan, 6 jiao in the bank, and 1,814 yuan, 2 jiao in silver rice. (2) There are 6,514 dan and 20 jin of grain stored. (3) The grain is suspected to have come from donations from gentry and merchants in urban and rural areas. (4) Measures to establish rural and town granaries have been ordered by the county magistrate to be handled by the various district offices.

The Provincial Office Orders the Selection of an Abbot for the North Temple. The North Temple in Suzhou is one of the ancient temples in Suzhou. The current monks of the temple, Zhao San and his disciple Jiu Hua, are competing for the position of abbot, resulting in various disputes. The county government hired local people to organize a committee to reorganize the North Temple and carry out the reorganization. However, the two monks have entrusted various major patrons to find ways to help them, and the dispute has not yet been resolved. Yesterday (the 21st), the county government received an order from the Civil Affairs Office to select an abbot for the North Temple immediately to resolve the dispute.

Battalion Commander Zhao Weixian is Arrested. Detailed account of the kidnapping of Wei Tingrong, the son-in-law of Zhu Bao San of Shanghai and a well-known figure in the French Concession. This newspaper previously reported on the incident of his escape. Wei has a brother-in-law, Zhao Weixian, who has repeatedly served in the military. Yesterday (the 21st), Zhao was suddenly arrested in Suzhou on suspicion of being involved in the case. The details are as follows: Four years ago, a Hunanese man named Zhao Weixian graduated from the École Libre des Sciences Politiques in France and then from the École Spéciale Militaire de Saint-Cyr, the highest cavalry school in France. After returning to China, he served in the Ministry of the Army when Duan Qirui was in power and was sent to Japan to observe. After completing the task, he became the chief instructor of the volunteer regiment in the French Concession. Wei Tingrong was the commander of the regiment, and the two got along well. That year, Zhu Bao San's ninth daughter married Zhao. Not long after, the volunteer regiment was reorganized into a volunteer team. Zhao and Wei had disagreements, and Zhao left the team, taking his family to Hankou. Later, he was the deputy commander of the special task force of the Fourth Division, went to Jiangxi to suppress bandits, and recovered Yushan. Now, Zhao is the battalion commander of the Sixth Water Police Battalion of the Ministry of Finance, stationed in Bengbu. Recently, due to the floods in Hankou, he took leave to go to Hankou to pick up his family and brought them to Suzhou, living at his mother-in-law's house at No. 3 Fuxing Bridge inside Xumen. It has been several days. Yesterday (the 21st) at 11:00 AM, Zhao received a telegram from Bengbu urging him to return to the battalion. Therefore, he bid farewell to his mother and wife and took a chartered car directly to the train station. Unexpectedly, Wei Tingrong's son, Mao Sheng, reported to the detective team that Zhao was the principal offender in Wei's kidnapping two years ago. The team sent detectives Wu Rongshan and others to arrest Zhao and take him to the team headquarters for interrogation. At that time, Mao Sheng led the way with a pistol in his hand. Afterwards, according to Zhao's wife (Zhu Bao San's ninth daughter), there was another background to this matter. It was also heard that Zhao is the brother of Zhao Hanying, a female calligrapher and painter, 31 years old. Huang Jinrong, a consultant to the Shanghai French Concession Police, heard the news that night and ordered someone to take a letter to the Suzhou Public Security Bureau, the content of which roughly stated that the suspect was of great value for research, and asked that he be strictly detained and that detectives be sent from the French Concession Police to Suzhou this morning to take him away.

Wuxi

The Ministry Orders Protection for Lixin Cloth. After the Wan case, when Lixin Textile Factory in Wuxi shipped its products to Shanghai, they were detained by the anti-Japanese association as Japanese goods. Although they were immediately returned after clarification, the time lost caused a lot of damage. Afterwards, the factory believed that at a time when domestic goods were being actively promoted, although the goods had trademarks and names for identification, they were afraid that there would be a recurrence of mis-deduction. Therefore, they specifically requested the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to protect them. The Ministry approved, "The presentation has been noted. We have informed the provincial governments to instruct their subordinates to facilitate the transportation and sales of domestic cloth in order to maintain it." At the same time, the provincial government ordered the counties to comply.

Anhui Rice Merchants Come to Wuxi to Buy Rice. Qian Zhongliang, the district chief of the First District, recently reported that rice merchants from Anhui Province have come to Wuxi to purchase large quantities of indica rice, as many as 200,000 shi, which will be shipped out soon. As a result, the price of rice has soared by more than three yuan, affecting the future of people's food supply. Yesterday, he specifically submitted a report to the county government requesting a strict ban on the export of rice and ordering the Rice and Bean Industry Association to lower the price of rice in order to maintain the people's livelihood and ensure social stability.

The Detective Team Arrests Thieves. The detective team of the County Public Security Bureau arrested two thieves, Zhu Guitian and Junru, on the road yesterday in connection with the robbery case at Bantang Temple. After being taken to the team, they were severely interrogated. According to their confession, they had previously shot and injured their accomplice, Qian Hai. This time, they had agreed with seven companions to go to Rongxiang in Kaiyuan Township to commit a robbery. The team obtained the confession and has prepared a document to send them to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

A Young Girl Dies After Falling From a Building. Xu Rongda, a resident of No. 2 Yingqiao Lane in the city of this county, is 27 years old and works as a silversmith in the Lao Renjin Jewelry Store in the North Gate. He has some savings and has not yet married. Last winter, he roamed around Zhou Shanbang and met a female worker from a silk factory named Miao Xiudi (also known as Miss Er), 19 years old, who lived in a nearby workshop. Unexpectedly, after a few dates, she became pregnant. However, the girl had already been betrothed to the son of the Liu family in Liutanqiao in this township. This spring, the matter was discovered by the Liu family, who forcibly took Xiudi home and forced her to marry. Xiudi was unwilling to live in the Liu family for a long time. Recently, she took advantage of an unguarded moment to sneak away and came to the city to discuss with Xu about divorcing her husband. Later, Xu persuaded someone to negotiate with Liu, and Liu agreed to receive 180 yuan as the cost of the wedding. At this point, Xiudi and Liu were divorced. Xu Rongda and Xiudi then started to live together. Who knew that her beauty would be short-lived and disaster would strike. Three days later, Xiudi suffered unbearable abdominal pain. She jumped from the building to escape, but her fetus was injured and could not be saved. She passed away at 10:00 PM that night.

Changzhou

Detectives Stationed in Shanghai are Sniped by Bandits. Ni Gusheng, the captain of the detective team of the Wuyi County Government, recently sent detectives to Shanghai to arrest the notorious bandit Qin Ermao, which was a great relief to the people. Qin's gang still has accomplices in Shanghai. Captain Ni continued to send detectives Zhao Xilin and others to Shanghai to arrest a bandit named Shen. At about 7:00 AM on the 20th, Zhao and others were in front of the Yangshupu Foreign Settlement Bureau, preparing to arrest the bandit Shen. Unexpectedly, the bandits struck first, and Zhao Xilin was shot three times. Detective Huanxi was shot once, and passersby were also killed and injured. Captain Ni Gusheng heard the news that day and took a night train to Shanghai to investigate.

Disaster Victims from Liyang Come to Changzhou. More than 80 refugees from Liyang County arrived at the train station outside Zhongshan Gate in Wuyi. They said that the county was hit by a major flood, and the beans and crops were all submerged. They had no choice but to go out to find food. The refugees stayed overnight at the station and then went to Shanghai to find hard labor.

Danyang

Another Robbery and Assault Case Occurs in the Northern Countryside. Last night, many bandits armed with guns suddenly came to the home of Sun Daheng in Fengyi Township, Gaoqiao, in the northern countryside. They rushed in through the back door, grabbed Daheng, and demanded silver, but they did not succeed. He was burned by fire. The remaining bandits searched the house and fled with their loot.

A Wanted Criminal is Arrested in Shanghai. After the bandit disturbance in Wujiaqiao in the northern countryside in January of this year, the wanted criminal Zhu Jinhai fled far away and has not been arrested. Now, the criminal Zhu has opened a Zhongnan Bookstore in Shanghai under a pseudonym. Yang Qinggeng and others from the county detective team learned of this and reported it to the county government, who prepared a document and went to take Zhu back to Danyang. After Wang Cheng审 conducted an interrogation, the confession was cunning. He has now been detained pending investigation.

Jiangyin

Chengxi Automobile Has Already Been Test-Driven. The Chengxi Road was damaged by the flood. The Construction Bureau is rushing to repair it. The construction has now been completed. The entire road is scheduled to be opened to traffic on September 1. Today (the 21st), five small cars were first used to transport passengers from Xicheng. Each ticket cost one yuan. It took one hour and twenty minutes to travel from Cheng to Xicheng. However, at Tangtouqiao, because the bridge surface was being raised, it was necessary to change cars to Xicheng, delaying the trip by ten minutes. After the official opening of traffic on September 1 next month, each ticket will only cost eight jiao.

The Total Number of Flooded Fields in the County. This year's flood has caused disasters in all 14 districts of the county. The disaster situation has been reported to the county government by the district chiefs, and personnel have been sent to investigate separately. The investigation has now been completed, with a total of more than 290,000 mu of disaster-stricken fields. The average loss is about 70%. The county government has reported the total number to the provincial office for handling.

Prison Inmates Request General Amnesty. Inmates in prisons in Changxing County, Zhejiang Province, and Jiading County, Jiangsu Province, initiated an telegram to the Central Government because the National Government's order for general amnesty this year only applied to political prisoners and not to ordinary civil and criminal offenders, requesting equal treatment and also granting amnesty. They also telegraphed to prisons in various counties to proceed together. The entire population of Jiangyin Prison and Detention Center also sent an telegram to the National Government, the Legislative Yuan, the Judicial Administration Yuan, and the high courts of various provinces, calling for and requesting that they be treated equally.

Page 12

Gaoyou

The Repeated Rise in Rice Prices is Worrying. Since the opening of the Sanba in this county, nine-tenths of the fields in the four townships have been submerged. Therefore, although rice factories in this city have large quantities of rice in stock, they are regarded as scarce goods and arbitrarily raise prices. The general population is very alarmed. Most of the middle and lower classes have switched to eating flour. It is hoped that the local authorities in this county will quickly establish a food investigation committee, strictly prohibit the export of food, assess market prices, and not allow price increases in order to maintain the people's food supply.

Yangzhou

The transportation of water has somewhat stabilized. Distributing relief and recovering corpses in the Grand Canal. Due to prolonged clear weather, the water level is gradually receding. The local Red Swastika Society is raising funds to purchase dry rations. On the 19th, the society dispatched its relief team, exiting Xu Ning Gate and heading east to the breach outside Quekou Gate in the north. They counted approximately five to six hundred households of unemployed poor families and distributed aid to them accordingly. On the other hand, from Xu Ning Gate, they headed west to the area outside the Customs House to prepare for the distribution of relief goods. On the afternoon of the 20th, the society, due to insufficient funds for extensive relief efforts, held a special meeting to discuss solutions. They decided to seek assistance in the form of relief funds from the head office and various philanthropists. As for the handling of floating corpses found in the Grand Canal, local residents Ruan Lianzhong, Xu Tingsong, Yin Kejun, and others have gathered like-minded individuals to hire workers to recover and bury the corpses.

Telegrams regarding Ma Yuren's activities to plot rebellion were received by the Pacification Commissioner's Office. According to a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Liang Jian, "The magistrate of Funing County, Lu Jixi, has repeatedly reported that Ma Yuren is indeed planning to take advantage of the situation and has colluded with bandits Shi Bao, Tian San Da Wang (Third King Tian), Er Tu Huanzi (Second Earth Badger), and other gangs, gathering forces in the area of Shibadunzi (Eighteen Mounds) in Lianjing. It has also been discovered that a large group of pirates are gathering in Dalian, intending to land from the mouth of the Yellow River, hoping to launch a major offensive. Considering the need to prevent any possible problems, I have dispatched two battalions from the 96th Brigade, led by Regiment Commander Chen Maolin, to set off early in the morning for Funing to rigorously suppress them." Furthermore, according to a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Liang Jian, relaying a telegram from Brigade Commander Zheng Tingzhen, "The bandit leader Tu Han's troops, numbering approximately five hundred, with three to four hundred rifles, aboard dozens of small steamers and civilian boats, are entrenched in the area of Zhouji Tujiagou, and are heading towards the western part of the Huai River and West Lake, cutting off traffic to Huozheng. Today, I have dispatched Regiment Commander Cao Dianwen, leading two battalions of soldiers, two field guns, and two machine guns, to cooperate with the populace and Song Brigade, aboard two steamers, to conduct a joint land and water suppression."

Xiaoshan

Verdict announced on the "Corrosive Liquid Poisoning Husband Case". Lou Baozhen, the wife of Han Yuanchang, the owner of a copper and tin shop outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan, was accused of pouring corrosive liquid into a teapot, plotting to poison her husband, Han Yunsheng. The county court sentenced her to one year and two months in prison. The prosecutor, dissatisfied, appealed to the Higher Court. Lou Baozhen was escorted to Hangzhou. After a court hearing, the original verdict was overturned, and she was sentenced to three years and three months in prison.

Angry Tidal Bore in Qiantang River Swamps and Sinks Two Boats. The tidal bore in the Qiantang River has been exceptionally strong recently, with the river level rising sharply. On the morning of the 19th, two fishing boats were overwhelmed by the tide at Yujiatan. Five boatmen were swept away together, their whereabouts unknown. A truly tragic event.

Shaoshan Survey of Sand Field Acreage. The Zhejiang Sand Field Bureau, after dispatching personnel to various districts throughout the province to investigate the total acreage of sand fields, found that Shaoshan has a total of 38,458 mu (approximately 6,345 acres). However, there are still more than thirty mu that have not been registered. The bureau is currently devising measures to encourage registration gradually.

Ningbo

Extortion Attempt Failed, God of Wealth Thrown into the Sea. Li Zunying of Baidu Village, Fenghua, was a relatively well-off man. In June of this year, he was kidnapped by bandits, who demanded a ransom of several thousand yuan. Li's family, finding it difficult to raise such a large sum of money at once, were trying to find ways to do so. Unexpectedly, the bandits, after waiting for two days without receiving any reply, threw Li Zunying into the sea, drowning him.

Hangzhou

Opening of the Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway on Schedule. The Beijing-Hangzhou National Highway, from Hangzhou to the Jiangsu border, has long been open to traffic. However, the Jiangsu section had not been completed, causing delays until now. Yesterday, reliable information was received that the Jiangsu Construction Department has officially scheduled the grand opening ceremony for the entire road to be held on September 1st. It is also reported that the road was opened to Yiyang yesterday (the 21st). It would have been possible to reach Yixing directly, but due to the floods that have not yet receded in that area, it has been temporarily postponed for a few days.

Provincial Government Decides to Dismiss Foreign Employees. The Zhejiang Construction Department reported that there is currently no need to retain foreign personnel for various tasks. It was decided that the contract of the bureau's Chief Engineer, Mr. Blancou, is about to expire, and a decision needs to be made as to whether or not to renew it. Also, a decision should be made regarding other Austrian personnel. After the Provincial Government discussed the matter, it was decided that the contract should not be renewed. Yesterday, the Construction Department was instructed to terminate the contract as soon as the expiration date arrives. Furthermore, the appointments of Mr. Beaumeier and Mr. Anaya, whose terms of office are tied to the Chief Engineer's term, should be terminated simultaneously.

Anqing

Proposal to Use Salt Tax Savings for Disaster Relief. Before the end of the Qing Dynasty, when constructing the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, the provinces of Zhili, Shandong, Jiangsu, and Anhui increased the salt tax to serve as railway stock. During the reign of Emperor Xuantong, this salt tax was loaned to foreigners, and the funds were later returned to the provinces. Anhui Province received over 80,000 taels of silver. This money eventually came into the hands of Fang Luzhong, the former vice-chairman of the Sino-Foreign Famine Relief Committee, who deposited it. The principal and interest have now exceeded 300,000 yuan. Due to the severe flooding in Anhui Province, people from Anhui living in Tianjin have sent a joint letter proposing that these funds be used to provide disaster relief.

Request to Revise the Date of Confucius' Birthday. The magistrate of Quanjiao County submitted a request to the Civil Affairs Department, asking them to forward it to the Ministry of Interior, to revise the date of Confucius' birthday. He cited that the Guliang Commentary and the Records of the Grand Historian both state that Confucius was born in the tenth month, with the Zhou calendar beginning in the Zi month, which corresponds to August in the Xia calendar. The national calendar should still be based on October. If the dates are not revised, it would be tantamount to saying that Confucius was born in June of the Xia calendar. The Civil Affairs Department instructed him to provide detailed citations and resubmit the request for verification and forwarding.

Bengbu

Planning Post-Disaster Relief for the Flooding in Northern Anhui. The scale of the flooding in northern Anhui this time is unprecedented in the last hundred years. The disaster area covers eighteen counties, with millions of victims. Wails of sorrow are heard everywhere, and everyone is clamoring for food. The Anhui Office of the World Red Swastika Society has raised over 10,000 yuan in relief funds and has sent personnel to various counties to investigate and distribute aid. However, the autumn harvest is hopeless, and the days ahead are long. Therefore, gentry from Anhui's Linhuai, Suzhou, Bengbu, Fengyang, Huaiyuan, Shouxian, and other counties plan to work together and devise relief measures collectively. Recently, they discussed initiating the Anhui Northern Anhui Disaster Relief Association and will convene representatives from eighteen counties in northern Anhui to Bengbu to discuss organizational methods. The planned measures include: (1) providing work as a form of relief, (2) private fundraising to establish fair-price rice distribution, and (3) requesting the central government to allocate funds for joint relief efforts. These measures are currently being planned and implemented.

Rampant Banditry in Dingyuan. Dingyuan in northern Anhui has long been known as a bandit area. In the spring of this year, it was disturbed by the bandit gang of Jiang Guochang, known as "Three-Legged Jiang." Later, the troops of Ge Wucheng, the Third Brigade of the Second Cavalry Division, exerted efforts to suppress them, and the banditry was somewhat subdued. However, recently, with the rise of the green gauze tents (referring to the period when crops grow tall, providing cover for bandits), the bandits have become rampant again. The bandit stronghold is located in the fields southeast of the county seat. They go out to rob and kidnap people every day. A few days ago, bandits gathered several hundred people and suddenly surrounded the house of a wealthy man, Liu Changsong, in the southeast of Outang Town. Liu's security guards colluded with the bandits from within, opening the gates. The bandits rushed in, captured Liu, and forced him to hand over foreign banknotes. Liu firmly refused and was shot dead. His son was also kidnapped. The Liu family's security guards, totaling more than thirty people, had long been in contact with the bandits and left with them. According to estimates, the Liu family suffered losses of tens of thousands of yuan. The magistrate of Dingyuan County, due to the rampant banditry, has not dared to go to the area to investigate.

Suzhou

Suixi Town and Over Two Hundred Villages Submerged. Suixi Town is located at the border of Jiangsu, Henan, and Anhui provinces. The people have long suffered from the scourge of war and bandits. Since the beginning of summer, there have been continuous rains for months. Furthermore, the dams of the Lieshan Coal Mine have blocked the flow of water, causing the north, central, and south branches of the rivers to overflow without drainage. Water has accumulated to a height of over three feet on the plains, destroying all the crops and turning homes into ruins. Fortunately, the residents of the town built defenses day and night, preventing the town from being completely submerged. However, over two hundred nearby villages have been swallowed by the raging waves. Among the affected villagers, aside from those who were rescued and escaped, approximately sixty people have been drowned, and the loss of property is estimated to be over eight million yuan. It has been reported that the area suffered from severe hailstorms this summer, resulting in a reduced harvest of winter wheat, causing widespread panic among the people. Now, they have suffered this great calamity. If the authorities do not provide proper post-disaster relief, the potential for future problems is very deep.

Letter Received

Letter from Xia Jinsheng of Fengxian

To the esteemed editor,

I read the article "Fengxian Adultery and Abduction Case Scheduled for Trial" in the local news section of your August 2nd edition. It stated that my wife suddenly appealed to the county government yesterday, admitting to having committed adultery with Secretary Zhou, and that Chen arranged the sale for a price, etc. Upon reading it, I found it to be slightly inconsistent with the facts. After my wife, Zhang, ran away on April 11th, Chen Shiqian, the owner of Chen Yuanxing Egg Shop on Nanqiao East Street, filed a lawsuit. As for the sale for a price, it has been explained as a misunderstanding by local officials, and a request has been filed with the county government to allow the withdrawal of the lawsuit. I am afraid that the outside world does not understand the truth, so I am writing to request your newspaper to correct the facts.

Sincerely,

Xia Jinsheng, August 19th.

1930 National Education Expenditure Statistics

▲106,495,690 Yuan

Nanjing, 21st. The national education expenditure statistics for 1930 have been compiled. Higher education expenditure is 11,177,735 yuan (excluding administrative expenses for private schools). Provincial education expenditure is 44,323,743 yuan. County education expenditure is 50,548,091 yuan. The total expenditure is 106,495,690 yuan.

Ministry of Education Clarifies Three Ambiguities in the Education Association Law

▲Instructions to the Jiangsu Education Department

The Ministry of Education received a telegram from the Jiangsu Education Department, which stated: Previously, the Ministry of Education telegraphed that, in addition to the elected representatives of lower-level education associations, other members of the county/city education associations, and provincial education association supervisors and directors also have the right to be elected as officers. Currently, in the county education associations, where lower-level district education associations have been established, most only list the names of the representatives of the lower-level district associations when submitting the member rosters. If a non-representative is elected as an officer, and the name of this officer was not initially included in the member roster, should the name of this officer be added to the roster after being elected, or how should it be handled? Requesting instructions (1). Article 19 of the Education Association Law states that upper-level education associations have their direct lower-level education associations as members. Therefore, these members should belong to the lower-level education associations, not to the individual representatives of the lower-level associations. In the member roster, the member should be the name of the lower-level education association. Under each member name, list the names of the representatives. If the Education Ministry hasn't given clear instructions on this procedure, we do not want to presume the procedure. Requesting instructions (2). Furthermore, Articles 12 and 13 of the Education Association Law stipulate that the establishment of city, county, and provincial education associations requires the consent of more than half of the district/county education associations. However, after the organization is established, should the district/counties that did not agree be allowed to freely withdraw? Requesting instructions (3). The Ministry of Education clarified: (1) District education associations should prepare two copies of the member roster and submit them to the county education association for storage and verification. (2) Upper-level education associations should treat the lower-level education associations as members and the suggestion from the Jiangsu Education Department on listing the member association names is correct and approve to follow the procedure. (3) All district education associations within a county should be required to join the county education association. Those who do not agree should follow the majority and should not be allowed to freely withdraw. Please comply with these instructions accordingly.

Vocational Education Society Establishes a Business Administration Department

Business administration is a highly valued field of study in modern times. To cultivate talents in this area, the China Vocational Education Society has added a Business Administration Department to its vocational tutoring night school, in addition to the existing English, Japanese, and Bookkeeping departments. It is reported that Dr. Cao Yunxiang, the former president of Tsinghua University, director-general of the Industrial and Commercial Management Association of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and a specialist in scientific management, has been hired as the honorary director. Cao Yimin, a graduate of the Business Administration Department of LaSalle University in the United States, Luo Qingfan, a graduate of the Engineering Department of Purdue University in the United States, Zhai Kegong, a graduate of the Business Administration Department of Columbia University in the United States, Huang Puqi, who specialized in mechanical engineering in the United States and serves as the director of the Engineering Department of the China Vocational School and the manager of the Dalong Iron Works, and Gao Shiheng, the assistant manager of the Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, will serve as instructors for the department's courses on methods of increasing efficiency, industrial knowledge, personnel management, and safety equipment. The Society has also contacted the China Chemical Industry Society, Kang Yuan Can Factory, Huasheng Electric Factory, Yixin Toothbrush Factory, Wuhe Weaving Factory, Meiya Silk Weaving Factory, Dahua Iron Factory, and Datong Bookstore to arrange for graduates of the department to be employed to the extent possible. It is reported that the entrance examination for this department will be held on September 1st. Anyone with a junior high school diploma or above who is interested in working in factories and studying scientific management can register from today.

Approval for the Establishment of the Dongya Sports Academy

▲The first sports academy in the country to be formally established.

The Dongya Sports Academy on Luban Road, Lujiawan, Shanghai, has been developing rapidly and achieving outstanding results in recent years. The academy's affiliated high school sports teacher training program and the Boy Scout training program have already been approved by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau and the China Boy Scout Headquarters. The academy applied to the Ministry of Education for formal establishment of the specialty program last year. The Ministry sent personnel to investigate and found that the curriculum and structure were excellent, but the funding and equipment did not meet the legal standards and the application was not approved. After receiving the order, the academy actively prepared and applied to the Ministry of Education for formal establishment again this summer. The Ministry sent personnel to conduct another inspection and found the academy very satisfactory. It has now instructed the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau to approve the establishment. It is reported that, apart from the sports departments attached to universities, there are currently no public sports academies in the country, and this is the first private sports academy to be approved.

The Jinan University recruited a large number of new students this year. The university will post the list of new students. The list consists of 205 names. Selected candidates will be medically examined on the 25th and 26th. The final list will be posted after the medical exam.

Yu Tianguang Wins Student Tennis Singles Championship

▲Runner-up: Qian Yaobin ▲Third Place: Ma Anquan

—Yu Tianguang Wins Over Qian Yaobin in Straight Sets Yesterday in the Finals—

—6-3, 8-6, 6-3—

The young tennis star Yu Tianguang won the Shanghai Chinese Student Tennis Singles Championship yesterday by defeating Qian Yaobin in straight sets with scores of 6-3, 8-6, and 6-3. Qian Yaobin was the runner-up, and Ma Anquan had already secured third place the day before.

▲The Champion's Results

The student tennis tournament was sponsored by the East China Company. Forty-four players participated and followed an elimination bracket. The 4 players in the re-run bracket played a round robin to decide the champion, runner up and third place. Yu Tianguang won every round robin match as shown:

▲The Process of Winning the Championship

Yu and Qian had each won twice, so they faced each other in the final match yesterday. Yu defeated Qian in straight sets to win the championship.

▲The Situation on the Court

Yu served first and won the first game with a clean sweep of four points. He then won two more games in a row, taking a commanding lead of 3-0. Qian, after suffering this setback, also won a game with a clean sweep of four points. The score then became 5-2. Yu Tianguang, unhurried, won the first set 6-3.

▲The Difficult to Resolve Match

Qian improved his serving and won a game, seeming to regain momentum, leading 3-1. Unfortunately, he then lost three games in a row. Fortunately, he won two more games, still leading 5-4. At this crucial moment, he could not win again, allowing Yu to make it 5-5 and then 6-5. Yu then suddenly won three games in a row to win the second set 8-6.

▲The Situation is No Longer Favorable

Qian had already lost two sets, and the situation was no longer in his favor. Yu Tianguang took an early lead of 4-2. Although he then advanced one game to make it 4-3, he ultimately could not maintain it and lost again 6-3. Yu won with a total score of 3-0.

▲Comparison of Performances

In terms of stability, Yu was much better than Qian. Qian was less fiery yesterday, but because he was too cautious, his performance was actually worse. His double faults on serves often led to the loss of games that he had been winning, which was a great pity. The second set was very good. He often won against Yu with balls that were close or far away. Although he often wanted to block at the net, there were many times when there was an opportunity, but ultimately the lack of power led to ineffectiveness. Yu Tianguang's long shots were very commendable and strategic. In the third game of the third set, he used a very accurate diagonal shot to make Qian run around, exhausting him and eliciting applause. Yu also had fewer net touches than Qian, and it was not easy for him to turn a dangerous situation into a victory. His victory over Qian yesterday was still more than adequate.

▲Prizes for the Top Three

▲Runner-up: A Spoulding tennis racket with Spoulding's good quality string from Spoulding, worth 60 yuan, won by Qian Yaobin.

▲Third Place: A Spoulding tennis racket with Spoulding's Singapore string from the East China Company, worth 40 yuan, won by Ma Anquan.
