Free Talk

World Anecdotes

— Hai Ke

Rubber Industry in the South Seas

The rubber industry in the South Seas is exceptionally developed. If travelers take a train from Singapore to Penang, it takes seven hours. The area it goes through is over 300 miles. You can see continuous rubber trees from the train window. There isn't a minute that you don't see them. The number of rubber trees is imaginable.

Unexpected Luck

One day, a tourist came to an art shop in Geneva, Switzerland. He paid five shillings for a small, dusty, and dirty oil painting as a souvenir of his trip. When he went back, he wiped off the dust and was overjoyed. It turned out that the painting was actually the work of the great Italian painter G. Reni, which is not easy to find on the market. If it is sold to a connoisseur, he can make a small fortune.

A Person Without Pain in His Life

In a small village in Lincolnshire, England, an old man named Allen T. Vlleno died at the age of ninety-five. It is said that he never had any pain in his life and did not know what disease was. What a piece of luck.

Qing Daoren's Treat and Mao Heting's Departure from Beijing

— Zizai

Linchuan Qing Daoren has been away from his friends for eleven years. His sixty-fifth birthday is coming up in a few days. I remember when he was selling his art in Shanghai, he was good at being a guest, but never a host. One day, he was commissioned to write a piece and received a generous payment. He suddenly sent out invitations to his friends for a banquet at a restaurant. His friends were all surprised. The poet Yu Keshi wrote a poem to mock him, saying, "Selling books gradually brings the intention of being treated well, getting a treat is all a freebie. Eating at restaurants is only a momentary thing, it is easier to go on a trip than to stay at home." Daoren smiled when he saw it. The rhyme of Yu's poem comes from Mao Heting's poem about leaving Beijing. Around 1912, many scholars and officials lingered in the old capital. They were poor and had nowhere to return. Mao styled himself as a remnant of the old dynasty and formed a society with two or three poet friends. They drank and sang, agreeing that not accepting official positions from the Republic was noble. His name card was written with "Former Qing Fourth-Rank Beijing Official." Before long, he was appointed as the Superintendent of the Wenzhou Customs. Mao did not know what to do but reluctantly took the job. When he left the capital, a friend said at the station, "We are here to see off the remnant of the old dynasty leaving the mountains." Mao wrote a poem to explain himself, which contained four lines saying, "Writing articles cannot be sold for gold, people of this generation mostly give white eyes. To starve to death is only a momentary thing, it is easier to live alone than to support a family." It was a shameless self-explanation, and his heart was bitter. One day, Yu said to his family, "Life is getting harder and harder, we are suffering from this era, how can we get through it? In the future, we will not be able to manage it." His concubine said, "Unless we stop socializing and treating guests. If we want to live a long and stable life, we can only be vegetarian, which is the most economical. This way, we can save a lot of money." Yu imitated Mao's poem to explain it, saying, "Vegetable oil is cheaper than lard, fat people should not look down on skinny people. Eating vegetarian food is only a momentary thing, it is easier to live alone than to support a family." He picked it up casually, showing his skill.

My Views on Disaster Relief

— Tianxu Wosheng

The methods of controlling floods are as follows: Gun embanked floods, while Yu dredged ditches and diverted rivers. "Embank" means to block, and "dredge" means to deepen. He deepened the ditches to connect them to the rivers. Therefore, Yu was able to govern the world, while Gun failed after nine years of effort. Piling firewood to block the gourd dike and carrying soil to block the Mengjin ferry are merely superficial solutions, not addressing the root cause. Reading reports on water disasters, they all state that the water level is higher than the sea level, which is why breaching causes disasters. Water naturally flows downward, so the key is to guide it according to the terrain. Hence, the annotations in the Yi and Ji Model mention that the famous rivers of the nine provinces are connected to the sea. The explanation emphasizes that small channels lead to large ones, so water flows from ditches to gullies, then to streams, then to rivers, and finally to the sea. Therefore, Yu's method of controlling floods was simply to focus on dredging the ditches, which is what made him superior to Gun. Now, the focus is solely on the upstream, without considering the downstream areas. This is like a water pipe losing its key connection, and the underground drain is blocked, causing water to overflow into the courtyard. At this point, trying to block the source is futile; the only solution is to clear the blockage to allow drainage. Underground, there are existing channels, so one should not resort to harming one's neighbors. However, if the neighboring channels are also blocked, then joint effort is needed to clear the blockage, ensuring that the water flows through the main road's drainage into the Huangpu River before stopping. This will prevent the Huangpu River from backflowing. Now, there is discussion about opening dams, but it is being obstructed, like the situation where neighboring channels are blocked, causing panic. But if neighbors stand idly by and refuse to join in clearing the channels, then flooding will be unavoidable. Therefore, the current plan should be to quickly provide work relief, leading these disaster victims to rush to the downstream areas and cooperate with the local people to dredge the ditches, preventing the arrival of floodwaters. The method should be based on the system of craftsmen in the Zhou Rituals. One person's effort should only dig to a width of half a foot. Two people form a pair, working from top to bottom. The work of one pair, one foot wide and one foot deep, is called a "quanche." At the head of the field, it should be doubled, two feet wide and two feet deep, which is called a "sui," to store the water. Nine people form a well, with a space of four feet wide and four feet deep, called a "gou," to receive the downstream water from the "quanche" and "sui." Every ten li forms a "cheng," with a space of eight feet wide and eight feet deep, called a "xu," to receive the water from the "gou." Every hundred li forms a "tong," with a space of two "xun" wide and two "ren" deep, called a "hui," which directly connects to the river, and from the river, it flows into the sea. At the beginning, one should complete one li in a day as a model, and then the collective effort can be distributed to dredge the downstream areas. Every village and town should, at this moment, exert their efforts in the ditches. Then, even if the Ru and Han rivers were to be diverted to drain the Huai and Si rivers, the water can still flow from the ditches into the rivers and into the sea. This is the same principle as unblocking the underground drain mentioned above. With the effort of one person, only digging half a foot wide and one foot deep, moving forward without stopping, the success will be swift. If there are a thousand people working for a day, the distance covered will be almost like a military march. The excavated soil can be placed on the side to be used as embankments to protect the fields. Then, fields that could only hold one foot of water can now hold three feet. The water will be dispersed, reducing its force, and the massive flood will be transformed into small streams, flowing out through different routes, just as the disaster victims are divided into groups to work. This will not cause harm. In the future, if there is drought, this water can be used to irrigate the fields. This is the merit of the "Dao Ren" in the Zhou Rituals and is a good method. At this time, when the cries of grief are everywhere and people have no place to live and cannot find food, if one person leads ten people to dredge the ditches and channels, and the disaster relief funds are used as wages, simply deepening the existing field ditches and waterways downstream, it does not require special skills, and both superficial and fundamental solutions can be achieved. I don't understand why this approach is not taken, but instead, people lament the high water level compared to the sea, knowing that a great disaster is coming, but not devising a plan to manage it. They are imitating Gun and not learning from Yu. Is it true that those in power are confused, while the onlookers are clear? The rivers and seas do not reject small streams. I hope that those in power will not dismiss these words as irrelevant. Then, once the mobilization order is issued, the God of the River will surrender at the mere sight of it, and the benefits will last for a thousand years. It's not just for the immediate moment. (Que Chou)

New Dancing Record

— Yao Ying

A dance endurance competition was recently held in Paris. The winner was named Tat Shide Lai. He danced for a total of seven hundred and fifty-two hours. Also, Mr. Maimuren and the French girl Fulan danced together. As a result, they ranked first and won a prize of one hundred gold coins.

When they announced that they would no longer dance, the girl had already worn out twenty pairs of dancing shoes, and the young man had also changed eight pairs. The runners-up were a young dancing couple. They stopped the day before because his partner's hamstring was strained.

The music they danced to was accompanied by electrical phonograph records. They were allowed a fifteen-minute break every hour, day and night. In addition to the expense of the prizes, the organizers of this grand dance party had a surplus of one thousand six hundred gold pounds.

Brief Commentary on Famous Artists' Excellent Records

— Shaoqing

Recently, my asthma flared up, confining me to my humble abode. My mind was troubled and confused, and I didn't know what to say. Fortunately, a friend lent me dozens of new records from the Gaoting Company. After listening to them for ten days, my illness was cured. It's amazing that singing can cure illnesses! So, I wrote this brief commentary as a thank you to the doctor.

Yang Xiaolou and Hao Shouchun sing "Lianhuan Tao" together. They are evenly matched and have equal skills. One coughs out jade-like words, and the other roars like the wind and clouds. The dialogue is meticulous, making the listeners' faces light up with joy. Ma Lianliang and Shang Xiaoyun sing "Tan Mu Hui Ling" and "Sang Yuan Hui." They are eloquent and meticulous in their choice of words, avoiding the beaten path. They are truly extraordinary. Qiu Guixian, Shang Xiaoyun, and Wang Shaolou sing "Er Jin Gong" together. With voices like iron and copper, they interweave the evening breeze and the remnant moon. The palace and commercial tones compete, each displaying their talents. Xue Yancin's "Pan Si Dong" and "Hui Long Ge" are like beautiful women adorning flowers and lovely birds singing in spring. The wonderful sounds are natural and unadorned. Xue Yancin and Wang Shaolou sing "Mei Long Zhen" together. The tones are novel, and the flavor is profound. Xun Huisheng's new drama, "Huan Zhu Yin," uses ancient short-sentence poems to compose a "Si Ping Diao." The idea is novel, and the rhythm is beautiful. Innovators of new tunes can use it as a reference. Professor Liu Tianhua's solo performance on the Nanhu, "Bing Zhong Yin" and "Kong Shan Niao Yu," are original compositions, exceptionally precious. The wonderful thing is that the music contains emotion, refreshing and pleasing to the ear. In addition, there are Liu Baoquan's "Nao Jiang Zhou Dan Dao Hui" in Dagushu, which is慷慨激昂generous and impassioned, Bai Yunpeng's "Daiyu Feng Gao"纒綿悱惻 which is melancholic and moving, and Lao Wogua's "Quan Wawa," which is滑稽可喜 humorous and delightful. The story-telling songs include Shen Jian'an and Xue Xiaoqing's "Zhen Zhu Ta," Xia Hesheng's "San Xiao," and Wang Meiyu's "Yang Liu Qing," etc., which are宛轉動人 touching and moving. There are many other excellent records, too numerous to mention. They are all new releases from the Gaoting Company.

Travelogue of India (87)

— Linghua

The reason why Brahmins have power is not only their doctrine but also their external protective organization, which is the caste system. They use strict methods to form a political, religious, and social system, making it weak but inviolable. External religions cannot break it. This is quite strange. As for their doctrine, the vastness and extensiveness of the Huayan school, the mysteriousness of the Mahavairocana Buddha and various sutras, the peculiar and obscure concepts of multiple gods, one god, and no god, and the intricate and esoteric nature of the Vijnanavada and Dharmalaksana schools are all derived from Hinduism. Only the caste system is problematic. Indian Hinduism is a new image of the world. Who can question it? If a leader like Gandhi uses politics and economics, it is immeasurable.

Recently, many young people have wished to break their caste system, but I see that the arguments against it and in favor of the caste system also seem reasonable. The principle of not being thorough is why Mr. Lu Xin's great work has value. What shall I do with the doctrine of the Great White Cow?

However, our Chinese cows are all yellow and black, lacking white cows. If I return to China from India, I will definitely buy a white cow to bring back. The Great White Cow represents Indian civilization, which is quite laughable.

Indian youths also slightly advocate free love. However, they encounter a major obstacle, which is the bloodline theory of the caste system myth. Indians believe in gods and want to be close to gods, so they must emphasize lineage. Therefore, the Brahmin caste is the most noble, making it easier to approach the gods. Even if they are not of this caste, they cannot marry other races because their bloodline has been in contact with the gods for a long time, making it the most noble. However, as science advances in the future, it should be able to break this arrogance.

I am writing this section to describe the great power of the new Brahmin religion, which is beyond my expectations. I never dreamed of it because I have looked down on this religion for many years. After coming to India, I also despised its caste system and naturally sneered at its custom of valuing cows. However, after visiting Gandhi and rereading Gandhi's biography, and observing from various aspects of India, I felt moved and wrote this. If Indian culture can be revived like this, I think Chinese people should also pay attention to it. Do not be slaves to others, and do not be too superficial. Research must be deep and thorough in world culture and academics to contribute to construction. Older people should not be stubborn, and younger people should not be superficial. Then we will be close to success. There is a poem as evidence: The Great White Cow of Indian Civilization (detailed in the Lotus Sutra). Deep sorrowful vows release kindness and enmity. Where is the new image of the East today? Kick up wind and clouds, a pleasure continent. (Buddhist sutras, utopian society) Although Chu has only three households, it will destroy Qin. There is not a single Buddhist disciple on the earth. After reading Byron, I grieve for Greece. Stroking Shewei, I often wipe my scarf. (Byron, an English poet, admired Greek culture and helped it fight for independence and died.) A hundred feelings linger when reading Byron. A poetic heart and chivalrous bones are a natural endowment. Serving in the temple (Lengyan language) is to repay kindness. Uphold righteousness together to support the wheel of culture.

Storytelling and Helping Society

Woman, Woman (26)

— Yao Su Feng

Miss Ding also forgot to resent and be angry for herself, but she was more resentful and more angry for the wife of Xiao Rong who was dragged along in the muddy water. Looking at the extraordinary conflict between the cruel strong and the yielding weak, she finally ignited the fire of sympathy for the weak. She also rushed out, braving the rain, shouting, meaning to seek help from anyone. Qiu Zi also followed behind, screaming madly and running swiftly. But there was no obstacle to Xiao Rong's violence.

The sky was as dark as night, especially in the heavy rain, and this section of the road was so deserted that there was not a single pedestrian. Xiao Rong still dragged his wife forward with force, running forward aimlessly.

After walking hundreds of steps, Xiao Rong's wife on the ground no longer showed any signs of resistance, but at this time Xiao Rong did not feel anything other than his own anger. He was still dragging his wife forward, panting with anger, to the intersection.

Suddenly, a car sped past from the cross street. Although there were several horn warnings, it was useless to Xiao Rong, especially in the thunderstorm, the sky was as dark as night, so Xiao Rong was knocked down by the car.

Miss Ding was the first to see the occurrence of this new tragedy, and immediately ran over with Qiu Zi. The car had stopped, and the two people lying on the ground were lifted into the car, ready to be sent to the hospital. Although a lot of blood was found on Xiao Rong's body, Miss Ding had no pity for him, she only saw that Xiao Rong's wife had fainted, and she felt very sad.

Then, in the hospital, Xiao Rong finally received natural punishment and left this sinful world in extremely painful groans. Xiao Rong's wife, however, only suffered some fright and stimulation, and recovered after a few days of treatment.

Miss Ding got the news of Xiao Rong's death at home first—Qiu Zi had inquired about it—and secretly shed tears behind people's backs, crying for her own unfortunate experience.

Xiao Rong's wife could only return to Miss Ding's place again. Miss Ding seemed very pitying and apologetic to her, so she exchanged the diamond ring that Xiao Rong had given her for money, and gave her some clothes and other things, and sent her back to her home in Suzhou. Xiao Rong's wife kept shedding tears on one hand, but was very grateful on the other hand. However, this gratitude was something that Miss Ding's conscience dared not accept.

Soon, school started. There were two fewer students, Mr. Lu and Miss Ding. Li Wenyao made a phone call to the Ding's house on Tongfu Road, and the telephone bureau said, "The phone there has been removed."

Later, Li Wenyao went there himself once, but a sign for rent had been hung on the gate of the Ding's house. (The End)

Gold Standard Plunges Suddenly

▲ Retreats into the Eighty Taels Range

▲ Falls Sharply by Ten Taels and Seven Fens Yesterday, the 21st, the gold standard showed weakness again, the situation was weak, the decline was rapid, and the progress was slow. The market as a whole had a review of ten taels. As a result, it fell sharply by ten taels and more. People were panicked and eager to sell, almost like the silver market before. It opened slightly lower, and then the exchange rate loosened, the listed price did not change, and Yuankang, Xiangchang, etc. sold actively, so the price continued to decline. Finally, it fell into eighty-two taels. It stabilized at noon. The selling trend was even stronger in the later market, especially the exchange rate was quite firm, so British gold was 1.26875, both buying and selling were possible. Finally, the bank bought in at 1.275, so the gold price was even more tired, and suddenly broke into the seven hundred and eighty taels range, which was really unexpected.

Government Bonds: "19 Good", Consolidated Tax Bonds Rise 6-7 Jiao

Yesterday at the Shanghai bond market, spot transactions were scarce, and although the futures market was slightly more active, the overall market situation remained quite calm. This was because major buyers and sellers continued to be inactive. Regarding the trend of bond prices, although there were no new changes in the overall bond market environment and no large transactions by major players, retail purchases were relatively strong. As it was late in the month, short positions were also slightly covered, so the market showed some activity. However, the selling pressure was not as strong as before, resulting in a rebound in the prices of various bonds. However, the trend was moderate, with no significant fluctuations in prices between the morning and afternoon sessions. As a result, futures for "Consolidated 6% Customs," "Reorganization," "Disbandment," and "96" were sluggish with minimal price changes, while "19 Good," "Consolidated Tax," and "20 Customs" bonds rose by 6-7 jiao each. In addition, spot customs bonds rose by 2 yuan and 3 jiao compared to the beginning of the month. The total value of spot transactions was 5,000 yuan, and the value of futures transactions was 7.9 million yuan in the morning and approximately 5 million yuan in the afternoon, totaling nearly 12.9 million yuan.

Yarn and Cotton Markets Remain Lifeless

The yarn market rose in the morning but fell in the afternoon, with the trend remaining weak. The global cotton industry is exceptionally pessimistic, and the decline in Three Grades Yarn is intensifying, with heavy downward pressure. Most speculators are inclined to sell. As for major players, they are buying near-term and selling far-term contracts. The demand for spot yarn from the Sichuan group is still relatively strong. However, market sentiment has not been shaken because of the unfavorable environment and the difficult-to-reverse overall situation. Overseas markets lack significant upward momentum, so when prices rise, more sellers emerge. However, the yarn market is different from the cotton market and may be a bit more resilient.

▲Man-Label Cotton: Morning Good, Afternoon Bad. The Man-Label market opened with a slight increase in American cotton, with a weak trend and stable sentiment. However, actual sales were good and the market atmosphere was tighter. Prices for all months rose by 4, 5, and 6 qian. In the afternoon, news of a sharp drop in Three Grades Yarn weakened market sentiment, and prices for all months fell by 7, 8, 9 qian to 1 liang and 1 qian. The total transaction volume was 27,800 bales. Sales exceeded purchases by 1,050 bales, with Gongtai selling 750 bales and Changfeng selling 1,050 bales. Purchases included Meiji buying 1,650 bales, Tianlong buying 400 bales, Yiyu buying 550 bales, and Lichang buying 550 bales. The closing prices are recorded below:

| Man-Label Closing Price | Change | Open Interest | | Man-Label Closing Price | Change | Open Interest |

▲Yarn Sales: 3,300 Bales. Spot yarn sales remained strong. Total purchases by various groups throughout the day were 3,300 bales. Among them, fellow traders bought 450 bales of futures. Prices were stable. Among the out-of-town traders, Sichuan bought 2,850 bales, Qingdao bought 125 bales, Hankou bought 125 bales, Guangdong bought 180 bales, inland areas bought 100 bales, Tianjin bought 200 bales, Gaoyang bought 100 bales, and miscellaneous traders bought 30 bales.

Cotton Market Lacks Strength

The cotton market is particularly weak due to the relatively low prices of American and Indian cotton. Foreign firms are vigorously promoting sales in the market, but there is a significant lack of buyers. Manufacturers, aware of the surplus abroad, are apprehensive and adopting a wait-and-see attitude. As for American cotton, due to abundant production, its ability to rebound is weak, so major players continue to sell. According to Japanese sources, there are rumors of an additional 800,000 to 900,000 bales of American cotton production. If confirmed, there are concerns about drastic changes. Furthermore, a compradore from a certain foreign firm has disappeared due to poor business performance, leaving 50,000 bales of Indian cotton pledged at a certain bank. This cargo will likely be sold to Chinese factories at a reduced price.

▲Hankou-Label Cotton Drops 2-3 Qian. The Hankou-Label market opened with a slight increase in American cotton, with slightly stronger sentiment. Prices for all months rose by 5 fen to 1 qian. In the afternoon, the Japanese market was weak, major players sold, and the market fell sharply by 3.5 qian. The total transaction volume was 83,500 dan. Sales included Ruidai selling 16,800 dan, Yichang selling 2,100 dan, Yiyu selling 3,800 dan, Jifeng selling 2,100 dan, Xiesheng selling 2,100 dan, and Xincheng selling 2,000 dan. Purchases included Dafu buying 2,400 dan, Xinheng buying 1,400 dan, Tianjiang buying 2,400 dan, Rongxing buying 6,800 dan, and Taixing buying 3,000 dan. The closing prices are recorded below:

American Cotton Slightly Rebounds After Short Covering

▲American Cotton Rebounds 10 Points. Yesterday, American cotton was initially weak due to selling pressure, but later strengthened due to short covering and support from Wall Street. Futures rose by 8 to 11 points, and spot prices rose by 10 points. British cotton futures fell by 1 point, and spot prices fell by 4 points. Egyptian cotton spot prices remained unchanged. Indian cotton initially fell slightly following American cotton, but rebounded later due to short covering and better news from Liverpool. Pingguoer fell by 2.5 rupees, Aomula fell by 2 rupees, and Bailuoxi fell by 3.75 rupees. The original telegram is recorded below (dated 20th):

Grain: Heavy and Light Japonica Rice Fall by 3 Jiao

▲Southern Market: Yesterday, the sources of supply from various groups remained constant, and port stocks were still heavy. City and rural store sales, in this autumn heat, had few customers, and buyers were selective, taking only fresh goods. Heavy japonica and light indica rice fell by 3 jiao. Early rice prices were slightly reduced due to weak sales. High-quality Lu Yang and pointed rice were very scarce and showed slight firmness. Stale rice sales were sluggish and fatigued. Shady rice was scarce and demand was stable, leading to price stability.

▲Xin Zha: Yesterday, the rice market remained sluggish. Sources of supply from the interior continued to flow in. Recent arrivals were particularly abundant from Suzhou and Changzhou. Market sentiment was poor, and stocks were abundant. As of yesterday afternoon, there were over one hundred rice boats on the Suzhou River, with an estimated total rice stock of around 25,000 shi. Sales at various stores were even weaker. Opening prices for all types of rice were weak in the morning, with only Lu Yang pointed rice showing some activity.

Inquiries and Transactions for Foreign Rice

Yesterday, the foreign rice market showed a stable trend. Due to the small stock of foreign rice and a rebound in local demand, coupled with stagnant activity from out-of-town merchants and a lack of large-scale sales, the market showed no significant gains or losses. Yesterday, 1,100 bags of small ground rice were sold by local merchants at 13 yuan and 8 jiao per bag, and 120 bags of Saigon No. 1 were sold at 14 yuan and 8 jiao and 5 fen per bag. There were no other transactions. Although the prices of foreign rice in producing areas have fallen, they are still difficult to match Shanghai prices. Although foreign firms have been offering sales recently, there have been no buyers for high-priced offers, and low-priced telegrams have not been approved. Yesterday, Mitsui & Co. sent out a telegram for 700 tons of small ground rice for shipment in September at 6 taels and 4 qian and 5 fen. In addition, Tongxingtai approved the immediate shipment of 500 tons at 6 taels and 5 qian and 5 fen. However, due to the requirement of advance payment, no one inquired about it.

Flour Futures: Selling Pressure Intense

▲All Months Plunge Approximately 3 Fen

Yesterday, after the flour futures market opened, rumors resurfaced about the US lending money to purchase wheat. Sellers aggressively sold off, long positions became anxious and surrendered, and prices immediately dropped across the board. Later, factories and out-of-town merchants also sold. Although foreign wheat was quoted at 2-3 jiao higher, short positions also covered, but the downward trend did not abate. In the afternoon, a client with close ties to political circles sold, and the selling pressure intensified further. Closing prices were down 3 fen for the current month, down 2 fen and 2.5 li for September, down 2.5 fen for October, down 2.75 fen for November, down 2.5 fen for December, and down 2.75 fen for January.

Wheat Futures and Spot Prices Show Slight Decline

Yesterday's wheat market saw spot wheat factories adopting a wait-and-see approach. The local market offered over a thousand bags of wheat from Kunshan, Wuxi, Yangzhou, and Taicang, among others. The quality of the wheat was relatively high, but the selling price fell by 2-3 fen due to widespread rumors that the government's US loan was becoming a reality, leading to weak market sentiment. Wheat futures were also affected by this and declined after the market opened. Closing prices were down 4 fen for the current month and down 3 fen for September, October, November, and December. January was also down 4 fen.

Silk, Tea, Yellow and White Filature Face Difficulties in European Sales

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign firm silk market remained difficult to improve. Overseas markets saw active sales by raw silk factories as European silk weaving mills resumed operations after the summer break, but Chinese silk prices remained low. Although silk telegrams were forwarded to Shanghai, Chinese merchants lacked sufficient silk, resulting in few transactions. Yesterday, only Xinfu and others imported 20 bales of Shanghai white filature, and Kaili imported 10 bales of yellow filature, both at firm prices.

Tea Merchants Active in Law's Estate and Fine Eyebrow Tea Sales to France

Yesterday, the Shanghai foreign firm tea market saw renewed demand for treasure eyebrow green tea from Law's Estate such as Mouyuan and Tunxi in the French market. Yongxing, Xiehe, Jinlong, Tongfu, and other firms showed strong interest. However, Chinese tea merchants, aware of the thin inventory, were unwilling to lower prices for sales, so transactions were not very strong. Needle eyebrow and show eyebrow teas continued to be popular. Qimen black tea was also resumed by the English firm Jardine Matheson, but their assessed prices were harsh, and market prices fell by another 5-6 taels.

Sugar Market: Jardine Matheson Opens with 10,000 Bags

Yesterday, sugar market telegrams from producing areas showed that the price of Cuban spot sugar continued to fall by 3.125 compared to the previous telegram. New York sugar futures for September and December both fell by 3 points, March of the following year remained unchanged, and May also fell by 1 point. Java spot and futures sugar lacked price fluctuations. Transactions on the public market were quiet. The price of Dutch coarse sugar and white new goods remained at 11 taels, 6 qian, and 7.5 fen, while old goods were at 11 taels and 4 qian and 5 fen. 20-grade medium sugar white was at 11 taels and 1 qian, and inferior grades were at 11 taels. Demand was very limited. Jardine Matheson sugar saw a sudden easing of factory prices, and buying sentiment weakened further. B Mark prices fell to 11 taels and 1 qian, DY Mark to 11 taels and 9 qian, and AX Mark to 11 taels, 8 qian, and 2.5 fen. The market trend was stable. The company opened with 10,000 bags of DY Mark for September disposal at 4 yuan, 6 jiao, and 5 fen per day; B Mark at 4 yuan and 8 jiao and 5 fen; and HM Mark at 4 yuan and 3 jiao and 5 fen. Merchants' interest was very weak, and the trend was flat. Jinfa offered several hundred bags of coarse sugar white at 11 taels and 6 qian per yuan, and Zhenxiang offered it at 11 taels and 5 qian and 5 fen, with few transactions. The market appeared flat and lifeless.

Metals: English Galvanized Iron Prices Rebound

English galvanized iron has recently become more active, resulting in a considerable volume of transactions. Yesterday, a total of 800-900 dan were offered, with buyers mainly from Fujian and Tianjin. The Yangtze River route had no demand due to high water levels. Prices were 15 taels and 2 qian and 5 fen for 22-gauge, 15 taels and 7 qian and 5 fen for 24-gauge, 16 taels for 26-gauge, 16 taels and 5 qian for 28-gauge, and 17 taels for 31-gauge.

Social News

Indian Poisonous Snakes

— Fulan

Indian poisonous snakes have always been known throughout the world. Among them, the Russell's viper is found everywhere, whether in open fields, roadside jungles, or house corners. Its demeanor is indescribably frightening, but it is indeed a beautiful snake. Its color is a mix of dark brown and light brown, with rows of dark oval spots. Like other venomous snakes, it enjoys basking in the warm sun. Its temperament is lazy and fierce, and it is not afraid of people. Once it settles in a place, it will resist with all its might if you try to move it even a little. Its main food is rats. Generally, snakes destroy countless rats every year. In this respect, it seems that snakes are serving humans, because humans suffer great losses from rats. In short, no matter what kind of animal, no matter how venomous it is, it ultimately has some good to balance its sins. When people believe an animal is harmful to humans, they try every means to eradicate it; or when they believe an animal is beneficial to humans, they try to induce its breeding. As a result, they violate the principle of mutual restraint in nature, and ultimately harm themselves.

All reptiles are oviparous, but there are also several kinds, especially venomous snakes, tree snakes, and all sea snakes, whose eggs are incubated in the mother's body, so they are like viviparous animals. The Russell's viper is one of the most famous ovoviviparous snakes. A female viper kept in the museum of the Bombay Natural History Society successively gave birth to sixty-three small snakes, all wriggling and alive. Russell's vipers, when fully grown, are no more than five to six inches long. In addition, the saw-scaled viper rarely grows to more than one foot. However, this small creature harbors countless sins. Saw-scaled vipers are found all over India, especially in dry, sandy areas. Of those bitten by them, about 20% die. In several places, such as the cities of Bombay, the number of people who die from snake bites each year is indeed not small. This is mainly because snakes like to bask in open spaces.

Among Indian snakes, the saw-scaled viper is considered the most provocative, with a perverse temperament. The slightest movement near it will cause it to become aggressive, as if it wants to eat people. When kept in cages in museums, it will shake and chirp whenever people stand or walk past it, as if scolding them. These venomous snakes employ a very clever strategy when attacking, coiling their bodies into double loops, exposing only their heads. These loops are constantly moving and rubbing against each other, thus producing a rustling sound. On its flanks, it is covered with tin-like scales, with a serrated shape in the middle, hence its name, "saw-scaled viper." When its body moves, the protruding scales rub together, emitting a very audible angry sound, followed by constant chirping, rapid tongue flicking, and sudden head thrusts, making it look very frightening.

The color of the saw-scaled viper varies, usually completely harmonizing with its environment. Snakes in sandy areas often lie half-buried in the sand, their color indistinguishable from the sand, making it difficult to track them. There is also a brown tree snake, whose color and markings are very similar to the saw-scaled viper. The only way to distinguish them is to look at their heads. The head of the saw-scaled viper is surrounded by many small, human-shaped stripes, just like its body. As for the brown tree snake, its head is broad and flat, completely different from its back.

Some may ask whether there is a difference in the severity of poisoning when the above-mentioned venomous snakes bite people. No, every case depends on the amount of venom absorbed by the human body. Sometimes, when a snake strikes, no venom is injected, or the snake's venom has just been depleted, or the amount left is very small, insufficient to cause a reaction in the human body. In that case, even if a highly venomous snake bites a person, it will not have any effect. Conversely, even a completely non-venomous snake can sometimes bite a person to death. In India, there is plenty of evidence to prove that many people have been killed by completely non-venomous snakes. The biggest reason for this is fear. "Fear" kills faster than snake venom. Its vicious impact on the body is very rapid and can cause the body to feel the same effects as snake venom.

Originally, the primary function of snake venom is to overcome its prey. The secondary function is as a digestive juice and to eliminate toxins from itself or other snakes. However, we must know that such disinfection is not entirely complete, but rather like vaccination, where toxins are inoculated or transferred through injection. For example, the cobra can eliminate the venom of the Russell's viper, because no Russell's viper can kill a cobra. Conversely, someone once saw a large cobra kill an ordinary cobra. This is because the large cobra contained a lot of venom and its injection force was strong.

The toxic substance contained in snake venom cannot be dissolved in water or destroyed by sunlight. It is an extremely complex liquid that cannot be analyzed chemically. Once its venom enters the human body, it spreads very quickly, making rescue very difficult. Tying the limb above the wound to stop blood flow, or even implementing the ancient saying, "A brave man cuts off his wrist when bitten by a poisonous snake," may reduce or prevent the spread of poison to the whole body. However, when encountering a fatal dose of poison, these methods are of little use.

There are many remedies and spells for treating snake venom, and some people believe them to be very effective. In fact, being bitten by a venomous snake a few times is not necessarily fatal. In such cases, using a spell is just the spell having good luck. In science, a blood serum therapy has recently been invented that can be used as an antidote for the venom of certain snakes. From a medical point of view, this is the only way to treat snake venom. The production of this serum involves injecting a large amount of snake venom into the blood of a horse. The first injection is very small and has little effect on the horse. The last injection is almost ten times the amount originally sufficient to kill a horse, and as a result, the horse absorbs it without any harm. The serum made from the blood of this horse becomes a powerful antidote.

When Professor Calmette of the Pasteur Institute in Paris first created his medicine, he believed he had a cure for all venomous snake bites. However, it later proved not to be that easy, because each snake has a unique venom. The injection made with the venom of snake A can only be used for snake bites caused by snake A, not for snake bites caused by snake B or snake C. Only by collecting the venom of various snakes, preparing the serum separately, and applying them separately can treatment be successful. However, collecting this large amount of venom for injection into giant animals is indeed difficult, unless it is Russell's vipers and cobras, which are found everywhere in India. Recently, the Pasteur Institute in Kasauli has produced a serum made from a mixture of the venom of cobras and Russell's vipers, which has a good effect in treating any snake bite. However, if you encounter a snake bite, you should first tie the upper part of the wound before formally seeking treatment, just a towel is enough to use. This can prevent the venom from being immediately absorbed by the whole body. If the bite is on the hands or feet, the binding should be above the wrist or knee. At the same time, quickly call a doctor for help.

Market News

▲The Zhongyuan Bookstore, located at the southern end of Qipan Street and Wuma Road, declares that it is formed by the merger of the three major bookstores in Jiangzuo, Chongwen and Chongxin. It is said that during the anniversary period, in order to give preferential treatment to all sectors of the country, it has specially joined forces with major bookstores in Shanghai to gather tens of thousands of kinds of new and old books and hold an unprecedented large-scale invincible competition and sale. Regardless of domestic or foreign editions, all books are sold at particularly low prices, and real-dollar coupons and lucky draw coupons are given away. Such a sacrifice will surely make buyers happy.

It is now planning to expand and change to a limited company. The Marda Pharmaceutical Factory also trusts Mr. Cao very much and has decided to allocate a part of the funds to speed up its completion. It is expected that it will be realized soon.
